zmEditor.component.blog = {
    data: {},
    //设置项;
    setting: function (box) {
        var nowEdit = zmEditor.component.nowEdit();
        var blogCont = nowEdit.find('.zm-component-blog-content');
       	var blogDataType= blogCont.attr('data-type');
       	var tabs1List;
		//1布局
        //1.1背景设置
        var config1_c1 = [
        	{type: 'slider',element:blogCont,flag:{title:'博客条数',param:'blogNum',size: [1, 10]}},
            {type: 'slider',element: blogCont, flag: {title: "背景颜色",style: 'color', param: "backgroundColor",goal:'.zm-component-blog-box'}},
            {type: 'slider',element: blogCont, flag: {title: '边框颜色', style: 'color', param: 'borderColor',goal:'.zm-component-blog-box'}},
            {type: 'slider',element: blogCont,flag: {title: "边框线条宽度<sapn style='font-size: 12px;'> (px)</span>", style: "noTab_noColor", param:'borderWidth', size: [0,5],goal:'.zm-component-blog-box'}},
          	{type: 'slider',element:blogCont,flag:{title:'博客间距',param:'marginBottom',size: [0,50],goal:'.zm-component-blog-box'}},
            {type:'radius',element:blogCont,flag:{goal:'.zm-component-blog-box'}}
        ];

        //1.2图片;
        var config1_c2 = [
        	{type:'blogImgScale',element:blogCont,flag:{title:'图片位置',param:''}}
        ];
        //1.3博客刷新;
        var config1_c3 = [
            {type:'blogHidrefresh',element:nowEdit,flag:{title:'显示刷新控件'}}
        ];
        //1.4阴影
        var config1_c4 = [
            {type:'boxShadow',element:blogCont,flag:{title:'阴影',style:'normal',param:''}}
        ];

        var tabs1_c1 = zmEditor.component.setItems.config(config1_c1);
        var tabs1_c3 = zmEditor.component.setItems.config(config1_c3);
        var tabs1_c4 = zmEditor.component.setItems.config(config1_c4);

        switch (blogDataType){
            case "words":

                tabs1List = [
                    {title: "常规布局",content: tabs1_c1},
                    {title: "博客刷新",content: tabs1_c3},
                    {title: "阴影",content: tabs1_c4}
                ];
                break;
            case "picBlog":
                var tabs1_c2 = zmEditor.component.setItems.config(config1_c2);
                tabs1List = [
                    {title: "常规布局",content: tabs1_c1},
                    {title: "图片",content: tabs1_c2},
                    {title: "博客刷新",content: tabs1_c3},
                    {title: "阴影",content: tabs1_c4}
                ];
                break;
            case "timeBlog":
                tabs1List = [
                    {title: "常规布局",content: tabs1_c1},
                    {title: "博客刷新",content: tabs1_c3},
                    {title: "阴影",content: tabs1_c4}
                ];
                break;
        }

        var tabs1 = zmEditor.component.setItems.tabs_child_new(tabs1List);
	
		//2.标题
        var config2 = [
            {type:'blogControlAlign', element:blogCont.find('.zm-component-blog-title-a'),flag:{title:'文字布局',addTit:"文字布局",goal:".zm-component-blog-title-a"}},
            {type:'blogSetTitIcon', element: blogCont, flag:{title: '标题图标'}},
            {type:'slider', element: blogCont, flag: {title: '图标颜色',style: 'color', param: "fill"}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '图标高度(px)',param: 'height',goal:".zm-component-blog-title-icon>svg"}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '图标缩进量(px)',param: 'marginLeft',goal:".zm-component-blog-title-icon"}},
            {type:'blogTitle', element: blogCont.find('.zm-component-blog-title-a'), flag:{style: 'color', param: "color", content: '标题文字设置'}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '标题缩进量(px)',param: 'titPadding',size:[0,50],goal: ".zm-component-blog-title-a"}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '光标悬浮文字颜色',style: 'color',param: 'hoverColor',goal:".zm-component-blog-title-a"}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '标题上部高度(px)',param: 'marginTop',size:[0,30],goal:".zm-component-blog-title"}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '标题下部高度(px)',param: 'marginBottom',size:[0,30],goal:".zm-component-blog-title"}}
        ];

        var tabs2 = zmEditor.component.setItems.config(config2);
		//3.时间
        var config3 = [{type:'blogHidTime',element:nowEdit,flag:{title:'显示博客发布时间',style:'normal',param:''}}];
        var tabs3 = zmEditor.component.setItems.config(config3);
		
		//4.内容
        var config4_c1 = [
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '内容显示行数',param: 'blogScale',goal:".zm-component-blog-word",size:[0,20],callback:zmEditor.component.blog.public.scaleImg}},
            {type:'blogTitle', element: blogCont.find('.zm-component-blog-word'), flag:{style: 'mini', param: "color", content: '内容文字设置'}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '首行上部高度(px)',param: 'marginTop',goal:".zm-component-blog-word>p:first-child",size:[0,30]}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '首字母文字缩进(px)',param: 'textIndent',goal:".zm-component-blog-word"}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '内容行距(px)',param: 'lineHeight',goal:".zm-component-blog-word",size:[0,30]}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '尾行下部(px)',param: 'marginBottom',goal:".zm-component-blog-word",size:[0,30]}},
            {type:'blogControlAlign',element:nowEdit.find('.zm-component-blog-word'),flag:{title:'文字布局',addTit:"内容文字布局",goal:".zm-component-blog-word"}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '边距缩进量(px)',param: 'marginLeftRight',goal:".zm-component-blog-word"}}];
        var config4_c2 = [
            {type:'blogDetails', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '查看详情',param: ''}},
            {type:'blogControlAlign',element:blogCont.find(".zm-component-blog-viewMore"),flag:{title:'文字布局',addTit:"文字布局",goal:".zm-component-blog-viewMore"}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title:'查看详情缩进量(px)',param: 'titPadding',size:[0,50],goal:".zm-component-blog-Details"}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '查看详情颜色',style: 'color',param: 'color',goal:".zm-component-blog-Details",lttCallBack:zmEditor.component.blog.details}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '光标悬浮文字颜色',style: 'color',param: 'hoverFill',goal:".zm-component-blog-Details",lttCallBack:zmEditor.component.blog.detailshoverColor()}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '查看详情上部高度',param: 'marginTop',size: [0, 30],goal:".zm-component-blog-viewMore"}},
            {type:'slider', element: nowEdit, flag:{title: '查看详情下部高度',param: 'marginBottom',size: [0, 30],goal:".zm-component-blog-viewMore"}}];

        var tabs1List2 = [

        box.css({"width": "296px", "height": "730px"});

    //与后台交互获取博客数据
    getBlogData: function () {
//      var url = /blog_interface/shopBlog/queryByPage;
//      $.ajax({
//          async: false,
//          type: 'get',
//          url: url,
//          dataType: 'json',
//          success: function (e) {
//              console.log(e)
//              zmEditor.component.blog.data = e;
//          },
//          error: function (e) {
//              console.log(e.status)
//          }
//      });
           zmEditor.component.blog.data = this.localBlog;
    },
    //加载页面;
    getReady:function (ele) {
        var _this = zmEditor.component.blog;
        var data = _this.data.data;
        var cont = ele.find('.zm-component-blog-content');
        var type = cont.data('type');
        var num = 2;
        var str = '';
        switch (type){
            case "words":
                data.forEach(function (p1, p2) {
                    //var blog = p1.news;
                    var date = new Date(p1.fCreateTime).toLocaleString().replace(/:d{1,2}$/,' ');
                    if(p2<num){
                        str += _this.blogHtml($(p1.fContent).find('img').eq(0).attr('src'),p1.fTitle,date,p1.fContent,p1.fId);
                    }
                });
                cont.html(str).addClass('wordsBlog');
                ele.width('535px');
                break;
            case "timeBlog":
				data.forEach(function (p1,p2) {
                    //var blog = p1.news;
                    var date = new Date(p1.fCreateTime).toLocaleString().replace(/:d{1,2}$/,' ');
                    var option = {
                    	"read":p1.fReadCount==null?99:p1.fReadCount,
                    	"share":p1.fForwardCount==null?99:p1.fForwardCount,
                    	"collect":p1.fCollectCount==null?99:p1.fCollectCount,
                    	"like":p1.fLikeCount==null?99:p1.fCollectCount,
                    	"review":p1.replyCount==null?99:p1.replyCount
                    }
                    if(p2<num){
                        str += _this.blogTime(date,p1.fTitle,p1.fContent,option,p1.fId);
                    }
                });
                cont.html(str);
                ele.width('730px');
                break;
            case "picBlog":
                data.forEach(function (p1, p2) {
                    //var blog = p1.news;
                    var date = new Date(p1.fCreateTime).toLocaleString().replace(/:d{1,2}$/,' ');
                    if(p2<num){
                        str += _this.blogHtml($(p1.fContent).find('video').length>0?'blogVideo'+$(p1.fContent).find('video').eq(0).attr('src'):$(p1.fContent).find('img').eq(0).attr('src'),p1.fTitle,date,p1.fContent);

                    }
                });
                cont.html(str).find('.zm-component-blog-mediaBox').width(cont.data('picWidth'));
                //cont.html(str).find('.zm-component-blog-mediaBox').addClass('onlyPic');
                if(cont.hasClass('leftPic')){
                    if(cont.attr('data-picWidth')=='344'){
                        ele.width('1059px');
                    }
                }
                else if(cont.hasClass('topPic')){
                	if(cont.attr('data-picWidth')=='400'){
                		ele.width('579px');
                	}
                }
                else if (cont.hasClass('onlyPic')){
                    if(cont.attr('data-picWidth')=='800'){
                    ele.width('1142px').find('.zm-component-blog-box').css("display","none").eq(0)
                        .css({"display":"block"});
                    }
            }

                break;
        }
            cont.find('.zm-component-blog-date').attr('data-type','YYYY-MM-DD');
            cont.find('.zm-component-blog-title-icon').css({"display":"none"});
            cont.attr('data-blogNum',num).find('.zm-component-blog-word').children().removeAttr('style');
            ele.find('.zm-components-blog-blogPages').remove();
            ele.attr({'prop':'16a9','mainWidth':'1059'});
    },
    //blog添加条数;
    blogNumControl:function(ele,n){
    	var newNum = n;
    	var oldNum = ele.find('.zm-component-blog-box').length;
    	var blogData=zmEditor.component.blog.data;
    	if(newNum > oldNum) {
    		$.each(blogData.data,function(index, val){
    			if(index < newNum && index > oldNum  - 1){
                    var bgurl=$(val.fContent).find('img').eq(0).attr("src");
                    var box= ele.find('.zm-component-blog-box:eq(-1)').clone(true)
                        .attr({'data-title':val.fTitle,'data-sortid':val.fId})
                        .find('img').attr('src',bgurl).end()
                        .find('.zm-component-blog-bgImg')
                        .css("background-image",'url('+bgurl+')').end()
                        .find('.zm-component-blog-bgVideo>video').attr("src",bgurl).end()
                        .find('.zm-component-blog-title-a').text(val.fTitle).end()
                        .find('.zm-component-blog-date').text(val.fCreateTime).end()
                        .find('.zm-component-blog-word').text($(val.fContent).text()).end()
                        .appendTo(ele);
                         $('.zm-components-blog-blogPages').before(box);

    			}
    		})
    	}else{
    		for(var x=0;x < oldNum - newNum;x++){
    			ele.find('.zm-component-blog-box').eq(-1).remove();
    		}
    	}
    },
    //记录main宽度;
    boxwidth:null,
    //图片缩放比例;
    proportion:null,

        /*blog main宽高*/
        blogScale:function (w,h,component) {
            zmEditor.component.blog.boxwidth=w;
            component.attr({'mainWidth':zmEditor.component.blog.boxwidth,"prop":"16a9"});
            var cont = component.find('.zm-component-blog-content');
            var topPicture=component.find('.zm-component-blog-box');

            var mediaBoxTwo=topPicture.find('.mediaBoxTwo');
            var eleWidth=component.attr('mainWidth');
            var bologBoxHig=component.find('.zm-component-blog-upcont');
            var heightB=bologBoxHig.css("height");
            var prop=component.attr('prop');

            eleWidth==component.attr('mainWidth')?component.css({"width":component.attr('mainWidth')}):component.width();

                 }
           }

        /* blog设置图片比例 */
        blogImageScale: function(ele,obj){

            boderColor = zmEditor.component.setItems.slider(blogImg,{title: "边框颜色",param: "borderColor",style: "color"});

                var component= ele.parent();

            })
            //左侧按钮;
            leftRadio.on('click',function () {
                ele.removeClass('upRadio').addClass('leftRadio');
                blogImg=ele.find('.medialBoxOne');
                if(ele.hasClass('topPic')){

            var img = e.find(".zm-edit-news-img");
            img.on("click",function(){

                ul.slideToggle();
            });

            img.on("blur",function(){
                ul.slideUp();
                $(this).removeClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
            });

            ul.on("click","li",function(){
                var scale = $(this).attr('data-type');
                var proper= scale.split("a");
                var prope=scale.replace("a",':');
                var bologBoxHig=ele.find('.zm-component-blog-upcont');
                var heightB=bologBoxHig.css("height");
                img.html($(this).html()+'<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon_triangle" viewBox="0 0 1024 1024" version="1.1"><path d="M747.663515 904.661333L276.686869 512.487434 747.663515 120.242424v784.418909z"/></svg>').attr("data-type",scale);
                ele.find('.zm-component-blog-box').attr("data-type",scale);
                ul.slideToggle();
                img.removeClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover")
                component.attr("prop",scale);
                if(cont.hasClass('upRadio')){
                    mediaBoxTwo.css({"width":eleWidth-40+"px","height":(eleWidth-40)/proper[0]*proper[1]+"px"});
                }else{
                    medialBoxOne.css({"width":(parseInt(heightB))*proper[0]/proper[1]+"px","height":heightB});
                    mediaBoxTwo.css({'display':"none"});
                }
            });

            ul.mouseleave(function(){
                ul.slideUp();
                img.removeClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
            });
            //初始化图片框比例；
            var type=ele.find('.zm-component-blog-box').attr("data-type");
            var radioName="";
            switch (type){
                case "16a9":
                    radioName="16 : 9";
                    break;
                case "3a2":
                    radioName="3 : 2";
                    break;
                case "4a3":
                    radioName="4 : 3";
                    break;
                case "1a1":
                    radioName="1 : 1";
                    break;
                case "3a4":
                    radioName="3 : 4";
                    break;
                case "2a3":
                    radioName="2 : 3";
                    break;
                case "9a16":
                    radioName="9 : 16";
                    break;
                default :
                    radioName="16 : 9";
                    break;
            }
            img.find('span').html(radioName);
            return e;
        },

			var D=zmEditor.component.setItems.config([{type:'slider', element: ele.find('.zm-components-blog-blogPages'), flag:{title: '控件光标悬浮颜色',style: 'color',param: 'hoverFill',lttCallBack:zmEditor.component.blog.bloghoverColor()}}]);
			var E=zmEditor.component.setItems.config([{type:'blogControlAlign', element:ele.find('.zm-components-blog-blogPages'),flag:{title:'控件位置',goal:'.zm-components-blog-blogPages'}}]);
			var F=zmEditor.component.setItems.config([{type:'slider', element: ele, flag:{title: '控件上部高度(px)',param: 'marginTop',size:[0,30],goal:".zm-components-blog-blogPages"}}]);
			e.find(".zm-edit-components-Vtime-style").append(A);
			e.find(".zm-edit-components-Vtime-textConfig").append(B);
			e.find(".zm-edit-components-Vtime-layout").append(C);
			e.find(".zm-edit-components-Vtime-padding").append(D);
			e.find(".zm-edit-components-Vtime-margin").append(E);
			e.find(".zm-edit-components-Vtime-margintop").append(F);
			/* 初始化 */
			var _btn = e.find(".zm-switch-refresh");
			var goal = zmEditor.component.setItems.strings.future(ele,obj);
			var initJudge = goal.attr("data-judge-refresh");
			var wrap = e.find(".zm-edit-components-refresh-wrap");
			var blogPages=ele.find('.zm-components-blog-blogPages');
			if(initJudge == "true"){
				_btn.addClass("zm-switch-box-on");
				wrap.show();
			}else{
				_btn.removeClass("zm-switch-box-on");
				wrap.hide();
			}
			/* 事件 */
            _btn.on("click",function () {
				var goal = zmEditor.component.setItems.strings.future(ele,obj);
				var judge = goal.attr("data-judge-refresh");
                    if(judge == "true"){
                        if(blogPages.length>0){
                            blogPages.hide();
                        }
                        goal.attr({"data-judge-refresh":"false"});
                        wrap.slideUp();
                    }else{
                        blogPages.show();
                    if(blogPages.find('.zm-components-refresh').length==1){
                        ele.find('.zm-components-refresh')
                            .html(e.find('.zm-edit-news-icon').html()).find('.icon_triangle').remove();
                    }
                    goal.attr({"data-judge-refresh":"true"});
                    wrap.slideDown();
                }
			});
			return e;

		},

		refreshList: function(title,arr,ele){
    		var svg = this.svg;
            var dif =  ele.find('.zm-component-blog-content').attr('data-ref');
            var style1 =
				'<span>' +svg.refresh1+'<span>换一批</span></span>'+svg.san;

                '<span class="downPage2">' + svg.arrowL +'<span class="refresh">下一页</span></span>'+
				'</div>'+ svg.san;
            var e = $('<div class="zm-edit-components-titIcon">'
                +'<span class="zm-edit-text-title">控件样式</span>'
                +'<div class="zm-edit-news-icon blogindent">'+ (dif==='fir'?style1:style2)+'</div>'
                +'<ul class="zm-edit-news-icon-ul"></ul>'
                +'</div>');
            var ul = e.find('.zm-edit-news-icon-ul');
            var icon = e.find(".zm-edit-news-icon");

            arr.map(function(icon){
                liStr+=icon
            });
            ul.html(liStr);
            zmEditor.component.blog.bloghoverColor();
            icon.on("click",function(){
                $(this).addClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
                ul.slideToggle();
            });

                $(this).removeClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
            });

            	var page = ele.find(".zm-components-blog-blogPages");
                icon.html($(this).html()+svg.san);

                var type = $(this).index()===0?'fir':'sec';
                ele.find('.zm-component-blog-content').attr('data-ref',type)

            });
            return e;
        },

		Blogtime:function(ele,obj){
        var e = $('<div class="zm-edit-components-Vtime">'
            +'<div class="zm-edit-components-Vtime-onOff"><span class="zm-edit-text-title" style="width:130px; height:60px; line-height:60px;">显示博客发布时间</span><label class="zm-switch-box zm-switch-time"><span class="zm-switch"></span></label></div>'

            +'</div></div>'
        );

        var B=zmEditor.component.setItems.config([{type:'blogTitle', element: ele.find('.zm-component-blog-date'), flag:{style: 'color', param: "color", content: '时间文字设置'}}]);

        e.find(".zm-edit-components-Vtime-layout").append(C);
        e.find(".zm-edit-components-Vtime-padding").append(D);
        e.find(".zm-edit-components-Vtime-margin").append(E);
			/* 初始化 */
            var _btn = e.find(".zm-switch-time");
            var goal = zmEditor.component.setItems.strings.future(ele,obj);
            var initJudge = goal.attr("data-judge-time");
            var wrap = e.find(".zm-edit-components-Blogtime-wrap");
            if(initJudge == "true"){
                _btn.addClass("zm-switch-box-on");
                wrap.show();
            }else{
                _btn.removeClass("zm-switch-box-on");
                wrap.hide();
            }
			/* 事件 */
        _btn.on("click", function () {
            var goal = zmEditor.component.setItems.strings.future(ele,obj);
            var judge = goal.attr("data-judge-time");
				if(judge == "true"){
					ele.find('.zm-component-blog-date').hide();
                    goal.attr({"data-judge-time":"false"});
					wrap.slideUp();
				}else{
                    ele.find('.zm-component-blog-date').show();
                    goal.attr({"data-judge-time": "true"});

        //"时间样式"设置
        timeList: function(title,arr,ele){
            var dateBox = ele.find('.zm-component-blog-date').eq(0)
            var e = $('<div>'+
                '<span class="zm-edit-text-title">'+ title+'</span>'
                +'<div class="zm-edit-news-time"><span>2012-3-11</span>'
                +'<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="time_triangle" viewBox="0 0 1024 1024" version="1.1"><path d="M747.663515 904.661333L276.686869 512.487434 747.663515 120.242424v784.418909z"/></svg>'
                +'</div>'
                +'<ul class="zm-edit-news-time-ul">'
                +'</ul></div>'
            );
            var ul = e.find('.zm-edit-news-time-ul');
            var time = e.find(".zm-edit-news-time span");
            zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.transformation(time,dateBox.attr("data-type"))
            var liStr = '';
            arr.map(function(icon){
                liStr+=icon
            });
            ul.html(liStr);
            time.parent().on("click",function(){
                $(this).addClass("zm-edit-news-time_hover");
                ul.slideToggle();
            });

            time.parent().on("blur",function(){
                ul.slideUp();
                $(this).removeClass("zm-edit-news-time_hover");
            });

            ul.on("click","li",function(){
                time.html($(this).html());
                zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.transformation(ele.find(".zm-component-blog-date"),$(this).attr("data-type"));
                ele.find('.zm-component-blog-date').attr('data-type',$(this).attr('data-type'));
                ul.slideUp();
                time.removeClass("zm-edit-news-time_hover");
            });
            return e;
        },
        //时间转换格式;
        timePlugins: {
			/*
			 * transformation(): 转换时间;
			 *            _this: 目标对象(jq对象);
			 *           formar: 时间转换格式(暂用原始格式);
			 * */
            transformation : function(_this,format){
                switch (format){
                    case "YYYY/M/D":
                        _this.text(
                            new Date().getFullYear()+"/"+
                            (new Date().getMonth()+1)+"/"+
                            new Date().getDate()
                        );
                        break;
                    case "YYYY-MM-DD":
                        var M = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.autoAddZero(new Date().getMonth()+1);
                        var D = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.autoAddZero(new Date().getDate());
                        _this.text(
                            new Date().getFullYear()+"-"+M+"-"+D
                        );
                        break;
                    case "YYYY年M月D日":
                        _this.text(
                            new Date().getFullYear()+"年"+
                            (new Date().getMonth()+1)+"月"+
                            new Date().getDate()+"日"
                        );
                        break;
                    case "YYYY_str年M_str月D_str日":
                        var YYYY_str = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.numAutoStr(new Date().getFullYear());
                        var M_str    = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.numAutoStr(new Date().getMonth()+1);
                        var D_str    = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.numAutoStr(new Date().getDate());
                        _this.text(
                            YYYY_str+"年"+M_str+"月"+D_str+"日"
                        );
                        break;
                    case "YYYY_str年M_str月":
                        var YYYY_str = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.numAutoStr(new Date().getFullYear());
                        var M_str    = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.numAutoStr(new Date().getMonth()+1);
                        _this.text(
                            YYYY_str+"年"+M_str+"月"
                        );
                        break;
                    case "M_str月D_str日":
                        var M_str  = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.numAutoStr(new Date().getMonth()+1);
                        var D_str  = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.numAutoStr(new Date().getDate());
                        _this.text(
                            M_str+"月"+D_str+"日"
                        );
                        break;
                    case "YYYY年M月":
                        _this.text(
                            new Date().getFullYear()+"年"+
                            (new Date().getMonth()+1)+"月"
                        );
                        break;
                    case "YYYY/M/D H:SPM(12)":
                        var S = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.autoAddZero(new Date().getMinutes());
                        _this.text(
                            new Date().getFullYear()+"/"+
                            (new Date().getMonth()+1)+"/"+
                            new Date().getDate()+" "+
                            (new Date().getHours()>12?new Date().getHours()-12 : new Date().getHours())+":"+
                            S+
                            (new Date().getHours()>12?" PM" : " AM")
                        );
                        break;
                    case "YYYY/M/D H:S(24)":
                        var S = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.autoAddZero(new Date().getMinutes());
                        _this.text(
                            new Date().getFullYear()+"/"+
                            (new Date().getMonth()+1)+"/"+
                            new Date().getDate()+" "+
                            new Date().getHours()+":"+
                            S
                        );
                        break;
                    case "YY/M/D":
                        _this.text(
                            new Date().getFullYear().toString().slice(0,2)+"/"+
                            (new Date().getMonth()+1)+"/"+
                            new Date().getDate()
                        );
                        break;
                    case "M/D/YY":
                        _this.text(
                            (new Date().getMonth()+1)+"/"+
                            new Date().getDate()+"/"+
                            (new Date().getFullYear().toString().slice(2,4))
                        );
                        break;
                    case "D-M_e":
                        var M_e    = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.numAutoEnglish(new Date().getMonth()+1);
                        _this.text(
                            new Date().getDate()+"-"+M_e
                        );
                        break;
                    case "D-M_e-YY":
                        var M_e    = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.numAutoEnglish(new Date().getMonth()+1);
                        _this.text(
                            new Date().getDate()+"-"+M_e+"-"+(new Date().getFullYear().toString().slice(2,4))
                        );
                        break;
                    case "M_e-YY":
                        var M_e    = zmEditor.component.blog.public.timePlugins.numAutoEnglish(new Date().getMonth()+1);
                        _this.text(
                            M_e+"-"+(new Date().getFullYear().toString().slice(2,4))
                        );
                        break;
                    default :
                        alert("参数formar传入的时间格式不正确！")
                        break;
                }
            },
			/*
			 * autoAddZero(): 不足两位，自动补0;
			 *
			 */
            autoAddZero : function(num){
                return num >= 10? num:"0"+num;
            },
			/*
			 * numAutoStr(): 日期类型转换，数字转字符串;
			 *          num: 要转换的数值;
			 */
            numAutoStr : function(num){
                var numStr = num.toString();
                var newStr = "";
                for(var i = 0;i<numStr.length;i++){
                    switch (numStr[i]){
                        case "0" :
                            newStr += "零";
                            break;
                        case "1" :
                            newStr += "一";
                            break;
                        case "2" :
                            newStr += "二";
                            break;
                        case "3" :
                            newStr += "三";
                            break;
                        case "4" :
                            newStr += "四";
                            break;
                        case "5" :
                            newStr += "五";
                            break;
                        case "6" :
                            newStr += "六";
                            break;
                        case "7" :
                            newStr += "七";
                            break;
                        case "8" :
                            newStr += "八";
                            break;
                        case "9" :
                            newStr += "九";
                            break;
                        default :
                            alert(numStr[i]+"非数字！");
                            break;
                    }
                }
                //判断是否为月份,中间加"十"(例:二十三)
                if(newStr.length == 2){
                    var arr = newStr.split("");
                    console.log(arr)
                    if(arr[0]=="一"){
                    arr.splice(0,1,"十");
                    }else {
                    	arr.splice(1,0,"十");
					}
                    arr = arr.join("");
                    return arr;
                }else{
                    return newStr;
                }
            },
			/*
			 * numAutoEnglish() : 将月份转换为English形式;
			 * 			  month	: int类型，月份数值;
			 */
            numAutoEnglish : function(month){
                var month_Englist = "";
                switch (month){
                    case 1:
                        month_Englist = "January";
                        break;
                    case 2:
                        month_Englist = "February";
                        break;
                    case 3:
                        month_Englist = "March";
                        break;
                    case 4:
                        month_Englist = "April";
                        break;
                    case 5:
                        month_Englist = "May";
                        break;
                    case 6:
                        month_Englist = "June";
                        break;
                    case 7:
                        month_Englist = "July";
                        break;
                    case 8:
                        month_Englist = "August";
                        break;
                    case 9:
                        month_Englist = "September";
                        break;
                    case 10:
                        month_Englist = "October";
                        break;
                    case 11:
                        month_Englist = "November";
                        break;
                    case 12:
                        month_Englist = "December";
                        break;
                    default:
                        alert("月份转换失败，参数不正确！");
                        break;
                }
                return month_Englist;
            }
        },

        //图标样式设置;
        moduleList: function(title,arr,ele){
            var svg=this.svg;
            var e = $(
                '<div class="zm-edit-components-titIcon">'
                +'<span class="zm-edit-text-title">'+ title+'</span>'
                +'<div class="zm-edit-news-icon zm-edit-blog-icon">'+svg.not+'<span class="notspan">'+tempName+'</span>'+svg.san+
				'</div><ul class="zm-edit-news-icon-ul"></ul></div>'
            );
            var ul = e.find('.zm-edit-news-icon-ul');
            var icon = e.find(".zm-edit-news-icon");
            var liStr = '';
            arr.map(function(icon){
                liStr+=icon
            });
            ul.html(liStr);

            icon.on("click",function(){
                $(this).addClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
                ul.slideToggle();
            });

            icon.on("blur",function(){
                ul.slideUp();
                $(this).removeClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
            });

            ul.on("click","li",function(){
                icon.html($(this).html()+svg.san);
                if($(this).attr('data-type')=='not'){
                    ele.find(".zm-component-blog-title-icon").css("display","none");
				}else{
                ele.find(".zm-component-blog-title")
                    .find("svg path").attr('d',$(this).find("svg path").attr('d'));
                ele.find(".zm-component-blog-title-icon").attr('data-type',$(this).attr('data-type'))
					.css({"display":"table-cell"});
                }
                ul.slideUp();
                icon.removeClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
            });
            var tempPath = '',tempName = '';
            var blogTitile = ele.find(".zm-component-blog-title-icon").attr('data-type');
            switch(blogTitile){
				case "not":
                    tempPath = $(arr[0]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName = '无图标';
					break;
                case "ling":
                    tempPath = $(arr[1]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName = '菱形图标 ';
                    break;
                case "fang":
                    tempPath = $(arr[2]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName = '方形图标 ';
                    break;
                case "shuang":
                    tempPath=$(arr[3]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="双线箭头";
                    break;
                case "dan":
                    tempPath=$(arr[4]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="单线箭头";
                    break;
                case "biao":
                    tempPath=$(arr[5]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="镖状箭头";
                    break;
                case "yuan":
                    tempPath=$(arr[6]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="圆形图标";
                    break;
                case "shu":
                    tempPath=$(arr[7]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="竖线图标";
                    break;
				default:
                    tempPath = $(arr[0]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName = '无图标';
                    break;
            }
            icon.find('path').eq(0).attr('d',tempPath);
            icon.find('span').html(tempName);
            return e;
        },

        //"详情样式"设置
        detailsList:function (title,arr,ele) {
            var svg=this.svg;
            var e = $(
                '<div class="zm-edit-components-titIcon">'
                +'<span class="zm-edit-text-title">'+ title+'</span>'
                +'<div class="zm-edit-news-icon not">'+svg.not+'<a>'+tempName+'</a>'+svg.san+'</div>' +
				'<ul class="zm-edit-news-icon-ul"></ul></div>'
            );
            var ul = e.find('.zm-edit-news-icon-ul');
            var icon = e.find(".zm-edit-news-icon");
            var liStr = '';
            arr.map(function(icon){
                liStr+=icon
            });
            ul.html(liStr);

            icon.on("click",function(){
                $(this).addClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
                ul.slideToggle();
            });
            icon.on("blur",function(){
                ul.slideUp();
                $(this).removeClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
            });

            ul.on("click","li",function(){
            	icon.html($(this).html()+svg.san);
            	var viewMore=ele.find('.zm-component-blog-viewMore');
            	var Detail=viewMore.find('.zm-component-blog-Details')
            	if($(this).find('a').hasClass('not')){
                    viewMore.css("display","none");
            	}else{
                    viewMore.css({"display":"table","width":"100%"}).end()
                    Detail.html($(this).html()).css({"display":"inline-block","padding-left":"0","padding-top":"0","padding-bottom":"0","vertical-align":"middle"})
					.find("svg.icon").css({"width":"15px","height":"15px","fill": Detail.css("color")});
                }
                ele.find(".zm-component-blog-viewMore").attr('data-type',$(this).attr('data-type'));
                ul.slideUp();
                icon.removeClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
            });
            var tempPath = '',tempName = '';
            var blogTitile = ele.find(".zm-component-blog-viewMore").attr('data-type');
            switch(blogTitile){
                case "notHave":
                    tempPath = $(arr[0]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName = '无';
                    break;
                case "viewDetails":
                    tempPath = $(arr[1]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName = '[查看详情]';
                    break;
                case "viewBox":
                    tempPath = $(arr[2]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName = '查看详情';
                    break;
                case "read":
                    tempPath=$(arr[3]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="阅读";
                    break;
                case "readNow":
                    tempPath=$(arr[4]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="现在阅读";
                    break;
                case "more":
                    tempPath=$(arr[5]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="more";
                    break;
                case "both":
                    tempPath=$(arr[6]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="";
                    break;
                case "added":
                    tempPath=$(arr[7]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="";
                    break;
                case "pixel":
                    tempPath=$(arr[8]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="";
                    break;
                case "thickDouble":
                    tempPath=$(arr[9]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="";
                    break;
                case "circle":
                    tempPath=$(arr[10]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName="";
                    break;
                default :
                    tempPath = $(arr[1]).find('path').attr('d');
                    tempName = '[查看详情]';
                    break;
            }

            icon.find('path').eq(0).attr('d',tempPath)
            icon.find('a').html(tempName);
            return e;
        },

		/* 文本对齐*/
        controlAlign:function (ele,flag) {
            var e = $('<div class="zm-edit-text-horAlign zm-edit-item"><span class="blogtext">文字布局</span></div>').append(this.horAlign(ele,flag.goal));
            return e
        },
		/* 对齐方式添加*/
        horAlign:function (ele,obj) {
            var svg = this.svg;
            var e = $('<ul><li class="horAlignStyle">'+ svg.alignL +'</li><li>'+ svg.alignC +'</li><li>'+ svg.alignR +'</li></ul>');
            var iSelected = obj.goal?ele.find(obj.goal):ele;
            var alignType = iSelected.eq(0).css('textAlign');
            var li = e.find('li').addClass('bolg-align');
            switch (alignType){
                case "left":   li.eq(0).addClass('horAlignStyle'); break;
                case "center": li.eq(1).addClass('horAlignStyle'); break;
                case "right":  li.eq(2).addClass('horAlignStyle'); break;
            }
            e.find('li').on('click',function () {
                li.removeClass('horAlignStyle');
                var _this = $(this);
                _this.addClass('horAlignStyle');
                var iSelected = obj.goal?ele.find(obj.goal):ele;
                var index = _this.index(),type;
                switch (index){
                    case 0: type = 'left';   break;
                    case 1: type = 'center'; break;
                    case 2: type = 'right';  break
                }
                iSelected.css('textAlign',type)
            });
            return e
        },
        //博客选择;
        blogpict:function(data){
            //zmEditor.component.blog.data.data.concat(data);
            var nowEdit = zmEditor.component.nowEdit();
            var blogcont = nowEdit.find('.zm-component-blog-content');
            var blogpage=blogcont.find('.zm-components-blog-blogPages');
            var WPtogo=$('.zm-dialog-pageList');
            var newNum=data.length;
            if(newNum>50){
            }else{
                $.each(data,function (key,val) {
                    var list=parseInt(WPtogo.find('.zm-dialog-pageList-one:eq(-1)').children('.zm-dialog-serialNumber').html());
                    var box= blogcont.find('.zm-component-blog-box:eq(-1)').clone(true,true)
                        .attr({'data-title':val.fTitle,'data-sortid':val.fId})
                        // .find('img').attr('src',$(val.fSrc).find('img').eq(0).attr("src")).end()
                        .find('.zm-component-blog-title-a').text(val.fTitle).end()
                        .find('.zm-component-blog-date').text(val.fTime).end()
                        .find('.zm-component-blog-word').text(val.fTxt).end()
                        .appendTo(blogcont);
                        blogpage.before(box);
                        WPtogo.find('.zm-dialog-pageList-one:eq(-1)').clone(true,true)
                        .attr({'data-name':val.fTitle,'data-sortid':val.fId})
                        .find('.zm-dialog-serialNumber').html(list+1).end()
                        .find('.zm-dialog-pageList-title').attr('placeholder',val.fTitle).end()
                        .appendTo(WPtogo);

                });
            }
        }
    },

    //博客管理设置;
    blogEditor:{
        silder:{},
        blogManager:function() {
            // var pageArr = this.slider;
            $('.zm-dialog-box').remove();
            var svg = zmEditor.component.blog.public.svg;
            zmEditor.dialog.open('html/blog/zm-components-blogPageFull.html', function () {
                $(".zm-dialog-box").find(".zm-dialog-bg").remove();
                var pageList = $('.zm-dialog-pageList>li').addClass('zm-component-carousel-slideDataBox');
                var dataBox = '.zm-component-blog-box';
                var main = $('.zm-dialog-carousel-pageManage'),
                    content = main.find('.zm-dialog-content'),
                    pageBox=content.find('.zm-dialog-pageBox'),
                    list = main.find('.zm-dialog-pageList'),
                    input = list.find('.zm-dialog-pageList-title'),
                    setBox = main.find('.zm-dialog-carousel-pageSetBox');
                var nowEdit = zmEditor.component.nowEdit(),
                    box = nowEdit.find('.zm-component-blog-content'),
                    slide = box.find('.zm-component-blog-box');
                var slideArr =slide.toArray();
                var listStr = '';
                //添加滚动条;
                content.mCustomScrollbar('destroy');//把content的滚动条删除;
                pageBox.mCustomScrollbar({theme:'minimal'});//给pageBox添加滚动条;
                slideArr.forEach(function (p1,p2) {
                    var slideDataBox = $(p1);
                    var slideTitle = slideDataBox.attr('data-title'),
                        slideId=slideDataBox.attr('data-sortid'),
                        slideTime=slideDataBox.attr('data-time');
                    listStr += editSlide(p2,slideTitle,slideTime,slideId);
                });
                list.html(listStr);
                var onePage = list.find('.zm-dialog-pageList-one');
                onePage.eq(parseInt(box.attr('data-nowNum'))-1).addClass('itsSetting');
                var errorEle = $('<p class="zm-dialog-carousel-nameError zm-tooltip" '
                    +'data-zm-title="※禁止重名！">'+ svg.error +'</p>');
                list.on('mousedown','li',function () {
                    var _this = $(this);
                    _this.addClass('itsSetting').siblings().removeClass('itsSetting');
                    var thisName = list.find('li.itsSetting').attr('data-name');
                    box.find(slide).each(function () {
                        var $this = $(this);
                        if($this.find(dataBox).attr('data-title')===thisName&&
                            $this.find(dataBox).attr('data-show')==='true'){
                            box.boxSlider('showSlide',$this.index());
                        }
                    });
                });
                //blog单条设置隐藏;
               list.on('click','.zm-dialog-eye',function (e) {
                   e.stopPropagation();
                    var _this=$(this),parent=_this.parent(),key=parent.attr('data-show');
                   if(_this.hasClass('showKey')){
                       parent.attr('data-show',key.toBoolean()?'false':'true');
                       if(parent.attr('data-show').toBoolean()){
                           $(slideArr[parent.index()]).attr('data-show','true').show();
                       }else {
                           $(slideArr[parent.index()]).attr('data-show','false').hide();
                       }
                       newSlider(slideArr)
                   }else {
                       parent.find('input').removeClass('onFocus onError').val('')
                           .attr('placeholder',parent.attr('data-name')).blur();
                       _this.addClass('showKey').next().html(svg.setting).addClass('setKey');
                       parent.find('p').remove()
                   }
                   _this.html(parent.attr('data-show').toBoolean()?svg.eyeOn:svg.eyeOff);
                }).on('click mouseenter mouseleave','.zm-dialog-pageList-one',function (e) {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    var _this = $(this);
                    list.find('.zm-dialog-pageList-one').removeClass('itsSetting');
                    _this.addClass('itsSetting');
                    var type=e.type;
                    switch (type){
                        case "mouseenter":
                            _this.addClass('onlay');
                            break;
                        case "mouseleave":
                            _this.removeClass('onlay');
                            break;
                        case "click":
                            _this.siblings('.zm-dialog-pageList-one').removeClass('onlayclick');
                            _this.addClass('onlayclick');
                            break;
                        default:
                            break;
                    }
               });
                //blog页面重命名
                list.on('dblclick','input',function (e) {
                    list.find('li').removeClass('sliderDragLi onlayclick').addClass('wrong');
                    e.preventDefault();
                    var _this = $(this),parent = _this.parent(),
                        showSvg =parent.find('.zm-dialog-eye');

                    _this.focus().addClass('onFocus').removeAttr('readonly');

                    showSvg.html(svg.wrong).removeClass('showKey')
                        .next().html(svg.right).removeClass('setKey');
                })
                    .on('blur','input',function () {
                        var _this = $(this);
                        if(_this.hasClass('onError')){
                            return
                        }
                        rename(_this.parent());
                        list.find('li').addClass('sliderDragLi').removeClass('wrong');
                    })
                    .on('keydown','input',function (e) {
                        switch (e.keyCode){
                            case 37:
                            case 38:
                            case 39:
                            case 40:
                            case 46:
                                e.stopPropagation();
                                break;
                            default:
                                break;
                        }
                        if(e.ctrlKey){
                            switch (e.keyCode){
                                case 67:
                                case 86:
                                case 88:
                                case 89:
                                case 90:
                                    e.stopPropagation();
                                    break;
                                default:
                                    break;
                            }
                        }
                    });
                //设置内容
                list.on('click','.zm-dialog-setting',function () {
                    var tabindex=$(this).attr('tabindex');
                    var _this = $(this),parent = _this.parent();
                    _this.focus();
                    parent.addClass('itsSetting').siblings().removeClass('itsSetting');
                    if(_this.hasClass('setKey')){
                        setBox.show().offset({top:_this.offset().top});
                    }
                    else {
                        rename(parent);
                    }
                    return tabindex;
                })
                    .on('blur','.zm-dialog-setting',function () {
                        setTimeout(function () {setBox.hide()},200);
                    });
                //重命名和删除功能;
                setBox.on('click','div',function () {
                    var _this = $(this),index = _this.index();
                    var cloneEle,newName;
                    var theSlide = list.find('.zm-dialog-pageList-one.itsSetting'),
                        theInput = theSlide.find('input'),
                        theShowKey = theSlide.find('.zm-dialog-eye'),
                        theSetBtn = theSlide.find('.zm-dialog-setting');
                    list.find('.zm-dialog-pageList-one').removeClass('wrong');
                    switch (index){
                        case 0:
                            //重命名;
                            theSlide.removeClass('sliderDragLi onlayclick').addClass('wrong');
                            theInput.focus().addClass('onFocus').removeAttr('readonly');
                            theShowKey.html(svg.wrong).removeClass('showKey');
                            theSetBtn.html(svg.right).removeClass('setKey');
                            break;
                        case 1:
                            //删除;
                            slideArr.splice(theSlide.index(),1);
                            theSlide.remove();
                            break;
                        default:
                            break
                    }
                    if(index>0){
                        list.find('li').each(function () {
                            var _this = $(this);
                            _this.find('span:eq(0)').html(_this.index()+1)
                        });
                        newSlider(slideArr)
                    }
                    _this.parent().hide()
                });

                function rename(ele) {
                    var parent = ele.parent(),
                        setSvg = ele.find('.zm-dialog-setting');
                    var index = ele.index();
                    var input = ele.find('input');
                    input.removeClass('onFocus');
                    if(input.val()===''){
                        input.attr('placeholder',parent.attr('data-name'))
                    }else {
                        input.attr('placeholder',input.val()).val('')
                    }
                    var tempKey = false;

                    parent.find('li').not(ele).each(function (p1,p2) {
                        if(ele.find('input').attr('placeholder')===$(p2).find('input').attr('placeholder')){
                            tempKey = true
                        }
                    });
                    if(tempKey){
                        ele.append(errorEle);
                        ele.find('input').addClass('onError').removeAttr('readonly');
                    }else {
                        ele.attr('data-name',ele.find('input').attr('placeholder')).find('p').remove();
                        ele.find('input').removeClass('onError').attr('readonly','readonly');
                        setSvg.html(svg.setting).addClass('setKey').prev().addClass('showKey')
                            .html(ele.attr('data-show').toBoolean()?svg.eyeOn:svg.eyeOff);
                        slide.eq(index).attr('data-title',ele.find('input').attr('placeholder'))
                            .find('.zm-component-blog-title-a').html(ele.find('input').attr('placeholder'))
                    }
                };
                //添加内容;
                function editSlide(i,name,time,id) {
                    return '<li class="zm-dialog-pageList-one sliderDragLi clearFloat"'
                        +'data-show="true" data-name="'+name+'" dat-time="'+time+'" data-sortid="'+id+'">'
                        +'<span class="zm-dialog-carousel-onePageIndex zm-dialog-serialNumber">'+ (Number(i)+1) +'</span>'
                        +'<input class="zm-dialog-pageList-title" placeholder="'+ name +'" readonly>'
                        +'<span class="zm-dialog-eye showKey showKey">'
                        +svg.eyeOn+'</span>'
                        +'<span tabindex="'+ i +'" class="zm-dialog-setting setKey">'
                        + svg.setting +'</span></li>'
                };
                //博客组件拖拽排序;
                list.aDragSort({dragEle:'.sliderDragLi',rule:'tb',callback:dragSortCb});
                function dragSortCb() {
                    var newSort = [];
                    list.find('li').each(function (x) {
                    var _this = $(this);
                    _this.find('span:eq(0)').html(_this.index()+1);
                    console.log($(slideArr[x]).attr('data-sortid'))
                        console.log(_this.attr('data-sortid'))
                        for(var i in slideArr){
                        if($(slideArr[i]).attr('data-sortid')===_this.attr('data-sortid')){
                             newSort.push(slideArr[i])
                            }
                        }
                    });
                    newSlider(newSort);
                }
                function newSlider(arr) {
                    // console.log(arr)
                    var tempStr = '';
                    arr.forEach(function (p1) {
                        if($(p1).attr('data-show')==='true'){
                            tempStr += p1.outerHTML;
                        }
                    });
                    box.html(tempStr);
                };
                //时间排序;
                function bologdeTime() {
                    var blogcont=$('.zm-component-blog-content');
                    var list=[];
                    list=blogcont.find('.zm-component-blog-box');
                    var ux=[];
                    //循环提取时间，并调用排序方法进行排序
                    for(var i=0;i<list.length;i++){
                        var tmp={};
                        tmp.dom=list.eq(i);
                        tmp.date=new Date(list.eq(i).find('.zm-component-blog-date').html().replace(/-/g,'/'));
                        console.log(list.eq(i).find('.zm-component-blog-date').html())
                        ux.push(tmp);
                    }
                    //数组排序，支持年的比较;
                    ux.sort(function (a,b) {
                        var myDate=new Date();
                        var year=myDate.getYear();
                        if(a.date.getYear<year && b.date.getYear==year){
                            return true;
                        }
                        return b.date-a.date;
                    })
                    //移除原先顺序错乱的box内容;
                    blogcont.find('.zm-component-blog-box').remove();
                    //重新添加排序好的内容;
                    for(var i=0;i<ux.length;i++){
                        blogcont.append(ux[i].dom);
                    }
                };
                //排序方式;
                var icon=$('.zm-dialog-Icon');
                var random=$('.zm-dialog-random');
                icon.on('click',function () {
                    $(this).addClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
                    random.slideToggle();
                })
                icon.on('blur',function () {
                    random.slideUp();
                    $(this).removeClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
                })
                random.on('click','li',function () {
                    var index=$(this).index();
                    icon.html($(this).html()+svg.san).removeClass("zm-edit-news-icon_hover");
                    random.slideUp();
                    switch (index){
                        case  0:
                            break;
                        case  1:
                           //bologdeTime()
                            break;
                        case  2:
                            //dragSortCb()
                            break;
                        default:
                            break;
                    }
                });
                //选择博客资源;
                var checkBlog=$('.zm-dialog-check');
                checkBlog.on('click','.zm-dialog-check-button',function () {
                    zmChoiceRadio.choiceBlogger({multiple :'true', sortBy: '', descOrAsc: '', callBack:zmEditor.component.blog.public.blogpict});
                })
            });
        }

margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">互联网的方式如何运用在硬件上： 雷军说，七年前想做硬件公司，于是在互联网上号召几百万人进行头脑风暴。做硬件的难点在于失败意味着全盘皆输，需要在保证品质的基础上实现每周更新。小米最了不起的地方是用互联网的方式做硬件。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">不同于Apple的保密机制，小米给了用户参与的机会，类似于农家乐，把参与感放在了服务里。在中国，互联网要走群众路线，从群众中来，到群众中去。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: 800; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased;\">第二点：效率。</span></p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">坚持成本定价，零毛利。这种情况下，对效率的要求是极致的。为什么传统商业卖的越来越贵：10%成本用于Marketing， 50%给了销售的各个环节等等，于是大多数生意的效率极为低下。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">想挣钱，要么提高价格，要么偷工减料。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">那么如何提升效率呢？要把Marketing的成本降到零，把事情做到极致，只有极致的东西才能口口相传。最开始，做一款手机，卖1000万台，花1亿研发手机，卖10倍。小米如何做到极致？倒逼机制：做到一样的品质，卖一半的价格。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">雷军向观众展示了小米手环，称其为“No.1 in China, No.2 in the world”. 他提到生产电池耐用时间久且防水的电子手环的两点初衷。一是是因为市场上售卖的电子手环电池持久力一般仅不到一周时间，且一旦忘记充电常常就无法再启动；二是防水性能低。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">基于这两点考虑且在与团队不断探索下，小米公司最终实现了小米手环60天的电池持久力以及防水功能，且售价仅79人民币。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">雷军还提到了进入中国电子手环市场的考量，由于中外市场环境的不同，中国老百姓并不热衷于室外运动，国外电子手环一千多人民币的价格让多数中国消费者望而却步。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">而小米手环以成本价格且超越同等品牌性能的优势，让其很快占领了整个市场。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">对于小米手环的发展过程，雷军强调：毛利率越高的公司不一定越好，毛利率越高其实是一条不归路。因为许多公司为了提高毛利率都会从两方面考虑：提高价格与控制成本。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">提高产品价格就是在与用户慢慢变成敌人，一旦控制成本就会慢慢变成偷工减料。因此，如何做成一个伟大的公司，就要看该公司到底有没有勇气限制毛利率。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">口碑的本质是超越预期，价格低花样多都不能促成口碑，超越预期即是做到极致的标志。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">其实过去两年小米公司经历了增长瓶颈。只有电商的效率能撑起小米的模式，电商只占商品零售总和的百分之十，百分之九十的市场都进不去。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">很多人劝雷军卖得贵一点，但小米要做一家与众不同的公司，最终目的是要推动社会进步。在进入了七十多个市场后，坏的产品都被淘汰了，而好的产品做得就更好更长久。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">在增长客户源的过程中，雷军一直在思考怎么能够接触到90%的用户。小米公司开始尝试用互联网的方法做实体零售业，发现和电商成本差不多，甚至还更低，开一家火一家，每平米销售额达到了世界第二。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">转眼间，小米公司已经设立了70家小米之家， 每家都几乎是销售产业里的第一 。这是一种新零售方式，用互联网的方式做零售业。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">卖手机是低频行为，那么怎么能够让顾客有意愿进店更频繁？合适的品类组合。将低频组合成高频与品类丰富度十分重要。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">电商很在乎用户的频率 把每个产品做到感动人心、坚持成本定价、坚持到用户完全相信你：闭着眼消费转换率特别高，于是看到一件买一件。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">实体店的运作成本甚至比电商低。传统零售业商家会消失吗？小米的模式是线上线下相结合。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">小米之家三年之内目标是开到1000家 ，五年内收入突破100亿美金。互联网不仅仅是技术，更是要用电商的方式重新思考线下零售店，零售店仍然有核心竞争力，线上线下同价。</p><p class=\"text\" style=\"margin-top: 25px; margin-bottom: 25px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 14px; line-height: 24px; font-family: arial, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, MicrosoftYaHei, 宋体, 宋体, Tahoma, Arial, Helvetica, STHeiti; vertical-align: baseline; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased; text-indent: 28px; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0.5px; white-space: normal; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">雷军说，互联网不仅仅是技术，更是考虑商业的全新方法论：如何能够做到极致的用户体验，如何能做到极致的运作效率，结合这两点，能做的事情便非常多。</p><p><br/></p>",
